# Riftbound Card Database

Generated from `riftbound_cards_organized.xlsx`.

## How to use this file

- Use **Jinx Builder** first if you are building around **Jinx / Demolitionist Jinx**.
- Use **Legends** to choose a deck identity.
- Use **Champion Units**, **Units**, **Spells**, and **Gear** to find playable cards by type.
- Use **Banned Errata** before finalizing a deck, because a card may have updated text or may not be legal.
- The **All Cards** section at the end is the full readable card list.

## Sheet index

| Section | What it contains |
|---|---|
| Legends | Deck identity cards. |
| Champion Units | Champion unit cards that can be included when legal for your deck domains. |
| Units | Non-champion unit cards. |
| Tokens | Token cards. |
| Spells | Action/reaction and other spell cards. |
| Gear | Gear cards. |
| Battlefields | Battlefield cards. |
| Runes | Rune cards. |
| Signatures | Signature cards. |
| Banned Errata | Cards with banned status or errata listed in the source data. |
| Jinx Builder | Non-banned Fury/Chaos cards scored for Jinx-relevant text. |
| All Cards | Full readable card list. |
